</span><span class="token punctuation" data-token-index="0">}</span><span class="" data-token-index="0">

white-space: pre;"><span class="token keyword" data-token-index="0">class</span><span class="" data-token-index="0"> </span><span class="token class-name" data-token-index="0">LinkedList</span><span class="" data-token-index="0"> </span><span class="token comment" data-token-index="0">/* implements List&lt;E&gt;, Queue */</span><span class="token punctuation" data-token-index="0">{</span><span class="" data-token-index="0">
</span><span class="token comment" data-token-index="0">// Elements are doubly linked - forward and backword - to one another</span><span class="" data-token-index="0">
</span><span class="token comment" data-token-index="0">// Ideal choice to implement Stack or Queue</span><span class="" data-token-index="0">
</span><span class="token comment" data-token-index="0">// Iteration is slower than ArrayList</span><span class="" data-token-index="0">
</span><span class="token comment" data-token-index="0">// Fast Insertion and Deletion</span><span class="" data-token-index="0">
</span><span class="token comment" data-token-index="0">// Implements Queue interface. Supports methods like peek(), poll()</span><span class="" data-token-index="0">
</span><span class="token comment" data-token-index="0">// and remove()</span><span class="" data-token-index="0">
</span><span class="token punctuation" data-token-index="0">}</span><span class="" data-token-index="0">

Linked List </span><span class="token keyword" data-token-index="0">extends</span><span class="" data-token-index="0"> </span><span class="token class-name" data-token-index="0">List</span><span class="" data-token-index="0"> and Queue</span><span class="token punctuation" data-token-index="0">.</span><span class="" data-token-index="0">Other than operations exposed by the Queue </span><span class="token keyword" data-token-index="0">interface</span><span class="token punctuation" data-token-index="0">,</span><span class="" data-token-index="0"> LinkedList
has the same operations </span><span class="token keyword" data-token-index="0">as</span><span class="" data-token-index="0"> an ArrayList</span><span class="token punctuation" data-token-index="0">.</span><span class="" data-token-index="0"> However</span><span class="token punctuation" data-token-index="0">,</span><span class="" data-token-index="0"> the underlying implementation </span><span class="token keyword" data-token-index="0">of</span><span class="" data-token-index="0"> Linked List is
different from that </span><span class="token keyword" data-token-index="0">of</span><span class="" data-token-index="0"> an ArrayList</span><span class="token punctuation" data-token-index="0">.</span><span class="" data-token-index="0">

ArrayList uses an Array kind </span><span class="token keyword" data-token-index="0">of</span><span class="" data-token-index="0"> structure to store elements</span><span class="token punctuation" data-token-index="0">.</span><span class="" data-token-index="0"> So</span><span class="token punctuation" data-token-index="0">,</span><span class="" data-token-index="0"> inserting and 
deleting from an ArrayList are expensive operations</span><span class="token punctuation" data-token-index="0">.</span><span class="" data-token-index="0"> However</span><span class="token punctuation" data-token-index="0">,</span><span class="" data-token-index="0"> search </span><span class="token keyword" data-token-index="0">of</span><span class="" data-token-index="0"> an 
ArrayList is faster than LinkedList</span><span class="token punctuation" data-token-index="0">.</span><span class="" data-token-index="0">

LinkedList uses a linked representation</span><span class="token punctuation" data-token-index="0">.</span><span class="" data-token-index="0"> Each object holds a link to the next element</span><span class="token punctuation" data-token-index="0">.</span><span class="" data-token-index="0"> Hence</span><span class="token punctuation" data-token-index="0">,</span><span class="" data-token-index="0"> insertion
and deletion are faster than ArrayList</span><span class="token punctuation" data-token-index="0">.</span><span class="" data-token-index="0"> But searching is slower</span><span class="token punctuation" data-token-index="0">.</span><span>
</span></div></div></div><div style="background: white; padding-right: 105px;"></div></div>&ZeroWidthSpace;</div></div><div data-block-id="b2106e43-b177-452d-a554-3ac1672bf76a" class="notion-selectable notion-text-block" style="width: 100%;     .intercom-lightweight-app {
      display: none;
    }
